### Page 4



With edge screen technology, access people, 

information, and apps in a flash. 

To turn on the edge screen feature, start at the 

Home screen and swipe up for Apps. Then tap 

 Settings > 

 Display > Edge screen.

Apps edge

Create shortcuts to access frequently 

used apps.

People edge

See missed calls and message notifications 

from your important contacts. 

Smart select

Capture images and GIF animations. 

Access the edge

Swipe to view 

edge screen.

Drag a 

notification for 

more details.

voice dictations. Plus, quickly search for content 

on your phone and across the Internet.

Bixby button.

Charge up

To charge your phone, first connect the 

Adaptive Fast Charger to the USB cable, and 

connect the USB to your phone. Then plug the 

Adaptive Fast Charger into an outlet. Keep your 

phone plugged in until it reaches 100% battery. 

WARNING: Use only Samsung-approved charging devices. 

Samsung accessories are designed to maximize battery life. 

Using other accessories may invalidate your warranty and may 

cause damage. 

Steps to phone setup

Powering on and off

To turn your phone on, press and hold the 

Power/Lock button. Once it’s on, press and 

hold that same button to power it off.

The how-to basics

The screen basics

To turn on your screen, press the Power/Lock 

button, then swipe up onscreen to unlock it. 

To turn your screen off, just press the 

Power/Lock button.

Using the Xfinity Mobile app

The Xfinity Mobile app is preloaded on 

your phone. Consider it your control center 

to track your usage, manage your account, 

and ask us anything.
